### <a id="the-inductive-types-h-s-p-v">The Inductive Types H, S, P, V</a>

This section presents the [Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="329" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="333" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="341" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="353" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="367" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="374" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="379" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="384" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="391" href="Algebras.Signatures.html" class="Module">Algebras.Signatures</a> <a id="411" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="418" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1299" class="Function">Signature</a><a id="427" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="429" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5595" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a><a id="430" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="432" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="433" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="435" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="440" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="447" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html" class="Module">MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems</a> <a id="473" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="480" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="494" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="497" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="504" href="Varieties.Varieties.html" class="Module">Varieties.Varieties</a> <a id="524" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="525" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a> <a id="527" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="529" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1299" class="Function">Signature</a> <a id="539" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5595" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a> <a id="541" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="542" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="544" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#544" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="548" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="550" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="564" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="566" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="573" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="578" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="585" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html" class="Module">Varieties.EquationalLogic</a><a id="610" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="611" class="Argument">𝑆</a> <a id="613" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="615" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="616" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="618" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#544" class="Bound">gfe</a><a id="621" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="623" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="630" class="Comment">--open import MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems using (hfunext) -- public</a>

</pre>


Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.




#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphic closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

</pre>



#### <a id="subalgebraic-closure">Subalgebraic closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of a class of algebras that is closed under the taking of subalgebras is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

</pre>



#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of an class of algebras closed under the taking of arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3624" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3629" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3631" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3632" <a id="4124" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4125" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4127" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4129" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4093" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4131" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4133" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4134" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4135" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4136" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4138" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4139" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4141" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4143" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4145" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4093" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4147" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4149" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4110" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4151" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4153" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4110" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4155" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4157" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4159" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4162" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4169" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4171" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4172" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4172" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4174" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4174" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4176" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4178" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4186" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4188" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4189" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4191" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4193" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4172" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4195" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4197" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4198" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4199" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4200" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4202" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3634" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4203" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4205" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4207" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4209" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4172" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4211" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4213" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4174" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4215" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4217" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4174" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4219" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4221" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4223" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="varietal-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will denote it by `V`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4563" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="4568" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4570" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4571" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4573" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4573" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4577" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="4585" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="4587" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4591" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="4595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4596" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4604" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4606" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4607" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4631" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4633" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4635" id="5216" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4573" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5217" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5219" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="5220" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5222" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5224" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5226" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5173" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5228" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5230" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5232" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visou"></a><a id="5235" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5235" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a>  <a id="5242" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5244" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5245" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5247" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5249" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5257" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5259" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5260" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5262" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5262" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5264" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5266" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5274" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5276" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5277" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5279" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5281" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5283" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5285" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5286" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5287" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5288" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5290" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5291" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5293" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5295" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5297" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5299" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5301" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5262" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5303" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5305" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5262" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5307" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5309" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5311" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visow"></a><a id="5314" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a>  <a id="5321" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5323" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5324" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5326" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5326" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5330" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5338" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5340" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5341" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5343" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5345" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5347" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5349" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5350" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5351" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5352" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5354" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4573" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5355" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5357" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5359" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5361" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5363" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5365" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5326" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5367" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5369" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5326" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5371" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5373" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5375" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we represent formally what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="5727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5738" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5740" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5741" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5743" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5745" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5753" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5755" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5755" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5757" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5759" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5764" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5765" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5773" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5775" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5776" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5778" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5782" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5785" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5787" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5790" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5792" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5794" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="5804" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5805" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5806" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5808" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5808" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5810" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5812" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5813" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5814" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5805" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5815" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5817" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5805" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5818" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5820" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5808" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5822" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="5824" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5808" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="5827" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5827" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5835" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5837" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5838" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5838" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5840" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5842" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5850" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5852" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5854" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5855" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5858" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5838" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5859" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="5860" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="5862" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5864" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5827" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5872" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5872" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5874" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5876" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="5878" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5878" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5880" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="5882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5883" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5888" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5889" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5897" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5872" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5899" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5900" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5902" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5905" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5872" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5906" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5909" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="5911" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5922" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5878" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="V-is-closed-under-lift">V is closed under lift</a>

As mentioned earlier, a technical hurdle that must be overcome when formalizing proofs in Agda is the proper handling of universe levels. In particular, in the proof of the Birkhoff's theorem, for example, we will need to know that if an algebra 𝑨 belongs to the variety V 𝒦, then so does the lift of 𝑨.  Let us get the tedious proof of this technical lemma out of the way.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6391" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="6396" href="Prelude.Lifts.html#2674" class="Module">Lift</a>
<a id="6401" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6408" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6408" class="Module">_</a> <a id="6410" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6411" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6413" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6415" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="6423" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6425" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6425" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6427" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6429" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6434" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6435" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6443" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6445" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6446" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6448" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6451" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6452" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="6455" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="6463" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6467" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6469" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6470" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6470" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6474" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6482" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6483" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6487" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6489" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6490" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6492" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6494" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6470" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6496" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6498" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6499" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6500" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6501" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6503" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6506" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6507" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6509" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6425" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
       <a id="6518" class="Comment">------------------------------------------</a>
  <a id="6563" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="6568" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4658" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6577" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6470" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6580" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6583" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6585" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6586" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6588" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6590" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6591" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6593" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6595" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6598" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6600" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6601" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6603" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6425" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="6607" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6611" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6612" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4659" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a><a id="6617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6618" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6618" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6619" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6621" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6621" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6622" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6624" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6626" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="6632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6633" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4659" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a> <a id="6639" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6621" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6640" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6642" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6643" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4164" class="Function">lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="6664" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6618" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6665" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="7830" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7834" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7835" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a><a id="7840" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7841" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7841" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7842" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7844" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7844" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7845" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7847" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7847" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7849" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7849" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7852" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7854" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7856" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="7862" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7863" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7867" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7847" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7868" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7870" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7871" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3489" class="Function">lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="7884" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7849" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7887" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

First, `P` is a closure operator.  This is proved by checking that `P` is *monotone*, *expansive*, and *idempotent*. The meaning of these terms will be clear from the definitions of the types that follow.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P-mono"></a><a id="8319" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8319" class="Function">P-mono</a> <a id="8326" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8328" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8329" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8329" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8331" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8331" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8333" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8335" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="8343" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8345" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8345" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8347" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8347" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="8350" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8352" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="8356" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8357" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8365" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8329" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8367" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8368" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8370" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8373" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8329" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8374" class="Symbol">)}</a>

 <a id="9140" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8962" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9148" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9149" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3842" class="InductiveConstructor">pliftw</a> <a id="9156" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9156" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9157" class="Symbol">)</a>   <a id="9161" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9163" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3842" class="InductiveConstructor">pliftw</a> <a id="9170" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9171" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8962" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9179" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9156" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9180" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="9183" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8962" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9191" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9192" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3919" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="9198" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9198" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9199" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9204" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9206" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4001" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9212" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9215" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9215" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9217" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9219" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8962" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9227" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9228" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9198" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9230" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9215" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9231" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="9235" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8962" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9243" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9244" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4001" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9250" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9250" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9251" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9256" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9258" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4001" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9264" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9267" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9267" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9269" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9271" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8962" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9279" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9280" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9250" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9282" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9267" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9283" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="9287" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8962" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9295" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9296" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4083" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="9302" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9302" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9304" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9304" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="9306" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9308" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9310" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="9316" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9317" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8962" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9325" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9302" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9326" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9328" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9304" class="Bound">x₁</a>
 <a id="9332" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8962" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9340" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9341" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="9347" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9347" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9349" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9349" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="9351" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9353" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9355" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="9361" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9362" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8962" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9370" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9347" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9371" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9373" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9349" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

Similarly, S is a closure operator.  The facts that S is idempotent and expansive won't be needed below, so we omit these, but we will make use of monotonicity of S.  Here is the proof of the latter.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="S-mono"></a><a id="9604" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9604" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9611" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9613" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9614" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9614" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9616" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9616" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="9618" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9620" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="9628" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9630" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9630" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9632" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9632" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="9635" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9637" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="9642" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9643" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="9651" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9614" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9653" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="9654" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="9656" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="9659" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9614" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9660" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="9664" class="Symbol">→</a>       <a id="9672" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9630" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9674" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9676" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9632" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="9679" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9681" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="9682" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9683" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9614" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9684" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9686" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9616" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9687" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9689" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9630" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9691" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9693" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="9694" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9695" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9614" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9696" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9698" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9616" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9699" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9701" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9632" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a>

<a id="9705" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9604" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9712" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9712" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9716" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9717" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="9723" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9723" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9724" class="Symbol">)</a>            <a id="9737" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9739" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="9745" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9746" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9712" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9750" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9723" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9751" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9753" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9604" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9760" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9760" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9764" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9765" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="9770" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9771" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9771" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9772" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9774" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9774" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9775" class="Symbol">)</a>         <a id="9785" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9787" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="9793" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9794" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9604" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9801" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9760" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9774" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9806" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="10193" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10200" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10200" class="Module">_</a> <a id="10202" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10203" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10203" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10205" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10205" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="10207" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10209" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="10217" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10219" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10219" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10221" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10223" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10228" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10229" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10237" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10203" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10239" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10240" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10242" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10245" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10203" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10246" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="10249" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="10257" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10257" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="10270" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10272" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10273" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10273" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10275" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10277" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10285" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10286" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10203" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10288" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10290" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10205" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10291" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10293" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10294" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10296" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10298" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10273" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10300" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#4363" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10320" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10219" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10322" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10324" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10273" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10326" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="10328" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="10329" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10330" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10203" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10331" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10333" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10205" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10334" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10336" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10219" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="10340" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10257" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="10353" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10354" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10354" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="10355" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10357" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10358" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10358" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10360" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14513" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10362" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10364" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10364" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="10366" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14513" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10368" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10368" class="Bound">C≤A</a><a id="10371" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10373" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14513" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10375" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10375" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="10378" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14513" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10380" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10380" class="Bound">B≅C</a><a id="10383" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10386" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10388" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3151" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="10393" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10507" class="Function">sA</a> <a id="10396" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10411" class="Function">B≤A</a>

 <a id="11669" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10627" class="Function">S→subalgebra</a> <a id="11682" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11683" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11683" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a    <a id="11775" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11775" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="11778" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11780" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11692" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="11782" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#4363" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="11802" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10589" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="12482" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12264" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="12496" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12497" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12497" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="12498" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="12500" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12500" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="12502" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14513" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12504" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12505" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12505" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="12507" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14513" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12509" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12509" class="Bound">C≤A</a><a id="12512" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12514" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14513" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12516" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12516" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="12519" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14513" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12521" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12521" class="Bound">B≅C</a> <a id="12525" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12527" class="Symbol">=</a>

The next lemma would be too obvious to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="14179" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14164" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="14184" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14186" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1826" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="14194" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14195" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="14201" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="14211" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14213" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13898" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>



We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

  <a id="15039" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15014" class="Function">α</a> <a id="15041" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15043" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="15045" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15045" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15047" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15047" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15049" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15051" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15052" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14955" class="Function">h</a> <a id="15054" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15047" class="Bound">i</a><a id="15055" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15057" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15058" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15045" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15060" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15047" class="Bound">i</a><a id="15061" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="15284" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15284" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="15286" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15288" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="15290" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14718" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="15292" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="15294" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="15296" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14421" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="15300" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15284" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="15302" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15304" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3919" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="15310" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="15313" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15313" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15315" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15317" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8771" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="15324" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15325" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13518" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="15327" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13600" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="15331" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13596" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15333" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14664" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="15337" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15313" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15339" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13596" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15341" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13518" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="15342" class="Symbol">))</a>


</pre>



#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="15558" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="15565" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15565" class="Module">_</a> <a id="15567" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15568" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15568" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15570" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15572" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="15580" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15582" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15582" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="15584" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15586" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="15591" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15592" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="15600" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15568" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15602" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="15603" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="15605" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15608" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15568" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15609" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="15612" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="16851" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15620" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16857" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16857" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16861" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16862" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a><a id="16867" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16868" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16868" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16869" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16871" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16871" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16872" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16874" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16874" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="16877" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16877" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="16880" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16882" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16884" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="16889" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16890" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15620" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16896" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16857" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16900" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16874" class="Bound">pA</a><a id="16902" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16904" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16877" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this subsection with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P⊆V"></a><a id="17154" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17154" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="17158" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17160" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17161" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17161" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17163" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17163" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="17165" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17167" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="17175" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17177" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17177" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17179" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17181" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17186" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17187" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17195" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17161" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17197" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17198" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17200" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17203" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17161" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17204" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="17207" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17209" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="17210" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17211" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17161" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17212" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17214" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17163" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17215" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17217" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17177" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17219" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="17221" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="17222" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17223" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17161" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17224" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17226" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17163" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17227" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17229" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17177" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="17551" class="Symbol">→</a>     <a id="17557" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="17558" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17559" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17504" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17561" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="17563" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17506" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17564" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17566" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17504" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17568" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="17570" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17506" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17571" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17573" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17574" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="17575" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17576" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17504" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17577" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17579" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17506" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17580" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17582" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17520" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17583" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17585" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="17587" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="17589" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17520" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="17592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17496" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17597" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17598" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="17603" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17604" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17604" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17605" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17607" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17607" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="17612" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17614" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17616" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17154" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="17620" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17621" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="17627" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17607" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="17633" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="17643" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="17681" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17496" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17686" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17687" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3151" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="17691" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17692" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17692" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17693" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17695" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17695" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17696" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17698" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17698" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="17702" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17702" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="17705" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17707" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17709" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5009" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="17716" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17717" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17496" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17722" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17698" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="17725" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17702" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

<a id="17782" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17496" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17787" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17788" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="17793" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17793" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17795" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17795" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="17797" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17799" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17801" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="17807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17808" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17496" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17813" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17793" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17814" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17816" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17795" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We just proved that `SP(𝒦) ⊆ V(𝒦)`, and we did so under fairly general assumptions about the universe level parameters.  Unfortunately, this is sometimes not quite general enough, so we now prove the inclusion again for the specific universe parameters that align with subsequent applications of this result.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="18156" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="18163" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18163" class="Module">_</a> <a id="18165" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18166" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18166" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18168" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18170" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="18178" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18180" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18180" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18182" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18184" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18189" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18190" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18198" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18166" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18200" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18201" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18203" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18204" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18207" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18166" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18208" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18211" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="18219" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18219" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18225" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18227" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="18228" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18229" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18232" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18166" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18233" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18235" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18238" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18166" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18240" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18241" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18243" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18244" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="18245" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18246" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18166" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18247" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18249" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18252" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18166" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18253" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18255" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18180" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18256" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18258" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="18260" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="18262" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18180" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="18266" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18219" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18272" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18273" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="18278" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18279" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18279" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18280" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18282" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18282" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18283" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18285" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18287" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18293" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18294" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18298" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18299" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17496" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18304" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18305" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="18311" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18282" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18312" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="18316" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18317" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="18323" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18324" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4164" class="Function">lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="18345" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18279" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18346" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="18443" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="18452" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18452" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18457" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18459" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18398" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18461" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#4042" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="18463" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4658" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18472" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18395" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18474" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18475" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18478" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18166" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18480" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18481" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="18486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18452" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18491" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18493" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18494" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#7338" class="Function">lift-alg-≤-lift</a> <a id="18510" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18398" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18512" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18513" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18395" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18514" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="18517" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18405" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

 <a id="18523" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18219" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18529" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18530" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3229" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="18536" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18536" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18540" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18540" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18543" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18545" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18547" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5009" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18554" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18555" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18219" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18561" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18536" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18564" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18566" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18540" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

 <a id="18572" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18219" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18578" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18579" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a><a id="18583" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18584" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18584" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18585" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18587" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18587" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18588" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18590" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18590" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18592" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="18595" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18597" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18599" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18605" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18606" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18611" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17496" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18616" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18590" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18617" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18620" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18633" class="Function">γ</a>
  <a id="18624" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="18633" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18633" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18635" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18637" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4658" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18646" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18584" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18648" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18649" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18652" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18166" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18654" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18655" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18657" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="18659" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18587" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
   <a id="18664" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18633" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18666" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18668" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1826" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="18676" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18677" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="18683" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="18693" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18695" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18592" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove a result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19195" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="19202" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19202" class="Module">_</a> <a id="19204" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19205" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19207" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19209" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="19217" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19219" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19219" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19221" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19223" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19225" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="19226" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19228" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19228" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19230" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19232" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19237" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19238" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19246" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19248" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19249" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19251" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19254" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19255" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19258" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="19266" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19266" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19284" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19286" href="Algebras.Products.html#4222" class="Function">class-product</a><a id="19299" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19300" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19301" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19303" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19304" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19306" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19219" class="Bound">X</a><a id="19307" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="19309" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19311" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19228" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19312" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19314" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19316" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="19317" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19318" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19321" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19322" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19324" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19327" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19328" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="19330" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19332" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19228" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19333" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="19337" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19266" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19355" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19357" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4083" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="19363" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19628" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19370" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19371" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4610" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="19374" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19679" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="19379" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="19383" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="19655" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19628" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19662" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19664" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3919" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="19670" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19567" class="Function">psllA</a>

  <a id="19679" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19679" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="19685" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19687" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19689" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19689" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19691" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19693" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19694" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19394" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19698" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19689" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19699" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19701" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="19703" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19704" href="Algebras.Products.html#4023" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19707" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19709" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19228" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19710" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19712" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19689" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19713" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="19717" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19679" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="19723" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19723" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19725" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19727" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1826" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="19735" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19736" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="19742" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="19752" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19754" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="19760" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="19770" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

So, since `PS⊆SP`, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class `𝒦` belongs to `SP(𝒦)`.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="19903" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19903" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="19921" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19923" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="19931" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19932" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19935" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19936" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19939" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19942" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19943" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19945" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19947" href="Algebras.Products.html#4222" class="Function">class-product</a><a id="19960" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19961" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19962" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19964" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19205" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19965" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19967" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19219" class="Bound">X</a><a id="19968" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="19970" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19972" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19228" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19973" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19975" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19977" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="19978" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19979" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="19981" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19228" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19982" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="19985" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19903" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20003" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20003" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="20007" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20009" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15620" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="20015" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20003" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="20019" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19266" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a>
